GT Equivalence Verification (CRK4)

GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_q*A*log(c3*t + c4)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,A)= -0.1149290460\,A^2 \;+\; 0.06806555110\,A\;\log(0.2569297861\,t+1).
\]
So any matching candidate must be exactly “(constant)\(\cdot A^2\)” plus “(constant)\(\cdot A\log(\alpha t+1)\)”, with **no** other dependence on \(t\) (outside the log), **no** other dependence on \(A\) (e.g., \(|A|\), Max, rational in \(A\), extra powers), and no extra additive constants.

Now check candidates:

1) \(A c0 e^{c1\tanh(\cdot)} + A c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\tanh(\cdot)\): has exponentials/tanh terms; cannot become \(A\log(\cdot)\) and also has a pure \(t\)-term. No.

2) \(A c0/(c1 t+1)+ A^{c2}c3 + c4 + c5(\cdots)^ {c8}\): has rational in \(t\), constant term, and \(A\)-nonpolynomial term. Cannot reduce to \(A\log(\cdot)\) while also keeping \(-A^2\). No.

3) Linear/exponential in \(t\) plus \(A^{c3}\): cannot create \(A\log(\cdot)\). No.

4) \(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A^{c2}c3\log(c4 t+1)+ c5 t/(c6+t)\).
To match GT we’d need:
- \(A^2 c0 = -0.1149 A^2\) (ok by setting \(c0\)).
- A log term must be exactly \(0.06806\,A\log(0.2569 t+1)\). Here it is \(A^{c2}c3\log(\cdot)\). Set \(c2=1\), \(c3=0.06806555\), \(c4=0.2569297861\).
- But there is also \(A c1\) (must be 0 ⇒ set \(c1=0\)).
- And \(c5 t/(c6+t)\) must vanish for all \(t\) ⇒ set \(c5=0\).
Then candidate becomes \(A^2 c0 + A c3\log(c4 t+1)\), which can match GT exactly with \(c0=-0.1149290460\). **This matches.**

5) Uses Max(0,A), exponentials: GT is polynomial/log and valid for negative A too; Max introduces piecewise behavior. Cannot equal for all real \(A\). No.
